  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

<div class='spoiler'>
This answer contains spoilers…
<span class='spoilerAnswerText'>
<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  
    It depends on what you want to do, Kelsey ends up with Ren, it ends up shallow because everything is chosen for Kelsey since Kishan had to stay behind<a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">…more</a>
    It depends on what you want to do, Kelsey ends up with Ren, it ends up shallow because everything is chosen for Kelsey since Kishan had to stay behind and marry Durga. Disappointing really, just not written as well as I was expecting from previous books in the series. <a href="#" rel="nofollow noopener">(less)</a>
  
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>

    <div class="section firstReview">
      

<div id="review_357628502" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/357628502" />
    <a title="Colleen Houck" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1163228-colleen-houck"><img alt="Colleen Houck" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1425326771p2/1163228.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/357628502?book_show_action=true">Jun 28, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Colleen Houck" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Colleen Houck" href="/user/show/1163228-colleen-houck">Colleen Houck</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span> (Review from the author)

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_186372522" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/186372522" />
    <a title="Ava" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5832186-ava"><img alt="Ava" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/186372522?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ava" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ava" href="/user/show/5832186-ava">Ava</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5832186-ava?shelf=cover-lust">cover-lust</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5832186-ava?shelf=paranormal-romance-fiction">paranormal-romance-fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5832186-ava?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5832186-ava?shelf=owned">owned</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5832186-ava?shelf=paper-copy">paper-copy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5832186-ava?shelf=two-stars">two-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer186372522" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer61537549631801160"><i>This review contains <b>unmarked spoilers.</b></i><br/><br/>If you didn't know before, I used to be very in love with this series before I started getting into other young adult novels. I still enjoy the two first books in the Tiger's Curse series, but after that I started to hate them.<br/><br/>*purses lips*<br/><br/>Let's face it: everyone knew who Kelsey would end up with. If you actually thought that Colleen would try something different, you're wrong, and deep down you knew it. You could hope all you want, but authors rarely take </span>
  <span id="freeText61537549631801160" style="display:none"><i>This review contains <b>unmarked spoilers.</b></i><br><br>If you didn't know before, I used to be very in love with this series before I started getting into other young adult novels. I still enjoy the two first books in the Tiger's Curse series, but after that I started to hate them.<br><br>*purses lips*<br><br>Let's face it: everyone knew who Kelsey would end up with. If you actually thought that Colleen would try something different, you're wrong, and deep down you knew it. You could hope all you want, but authors rarely take the surprising side out of a love triangle. So ask yourself, and don't be bias:<br><br>Who would end up with Kelsey in the end?<br><br>Ren, <i>duh</i>.<br><br>That was no surprise, but I wasn't expecting that <i>ending.</i> I'm absolutely livid, and I'm not very thrilled about it, mind you.<br><br><b>Plot</b><br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9284655.Tiger_s_Curse__The_Tiger_Saga___1_" title="Tiger's Curse (The Tiger Saga, #1) by Colleen Houck" rel="nofollow noopener">TIGER'S CURSE</a> was truly amazing. It remains one of my favorite guilty-pleasure books.<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/9662386.Tiger_s_Quest__The_Tiger_Saga___2_" title="Tiger's Quest (The Tiger Saga, #2) by Colleen Houck" rel="nofollow noopener">TIGER'S QUEST</a> I adored even more, because the plot was great and kISHAN IS SUCH A BABE.<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7849341.Tiger_s_Voyage__The_Tiger_Saga___3_" title="Tiger's Voyage (The Tiger Saga, #3) by Colleen Houck" rel="nofollow noopener">TIGER'S VOYAGE</a> left me raging. Suddenly, Kelsey's become one of YA's worst heroines, and Ren and Kishan have have completely changed to adjust to her 'type'.<br><br>TIGER'S DESTINY was undeniably better - at least until the ending - but it was still a train wreck. TIGER'S DESTINY begins with Kelsey, who's cruising on the damsel in distress ship. She's been captured by Lokesh, and while Colleen tries to make Kelsey the ultimate kickass deceiver, it comes off as rather pathetic, since we see it from Kelsey's point of view. <br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/we%20got%20a%20badass/1nt3rc3pt0r/Meme/watch-out-we-got-a-badass-over-here-meme.png?o=0" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380353443i/706789.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Anyway, Kelsey is rescued by her <s>slaves</s> boyfriend and ex-boyfriend (who she's in love with) before Lokesh marries and beds her.<br><br>To break the curse, Kelsey has to retrieve the Rope of Fire, and complete a bunch of quests. Along the way, there was a big surprise, Kishan and Durga started flirting with each other (it made me sick), Kelsey bitched about wanting Ren, there were that sounded like a rip-off of Lord of the Rings, and a whole bunch of time-traveling crap that made my brain hurt. <br><br>The book is definitely action-packed, containing a heart-wrenching death that made me sniffle and a good plot that would've been better if it wasn't all over the place. <br><br><b>Romance</b><br><br>One of my biggest pet peeves in the series is that every single creature in every universe is in love with or wanting or lusting after Kelsey. She’s also dumb enough to still think no one likes her.<br><br>And this girl. This girl is not even slightly interesting. The only word adequate to describe her is stupid. STUPID. <br><br>You'd think that almost three years after meeting Ren and Kishan, she'd know that the brothers think she's the world’s gift to mankind, and to shut the hell up with the 'I'm a demented Cabbage Patch Doll and he deserves a Barbie' shit.<br><br>But, I'm devastated to report Kelsey actually <i>goes back</i> to feeling bad for herself (I mean, her parents died. She doesn't deserve happiness, right?), thinking that she's too dull for Ren (she is, of course, but when she's been whining about it for four books straight, you just want to super glue her jaws), being annoying as hell, and a jealous, stupid bitch who makes about as much sense as Donald Trump's hair. <br><br>Now, there’s something I noticed that didn't make a lot of sense. She's not good enough for Ren, but Kishan is okay? Eh? Come again? That’s a slap in the face to poor Kishan, who’s heart gets trampled so many times, I would’ve gone mad (Match-Point style) and murdered Kelsey.<br><br>To any other girl, the answer to this love triangle would be obvious: Kelsey should let go of poor Kishan, who’s only going to get hurt by her stupidity. Kelsey goes back to Ren, and Kishan has a shot with somebody who’s not a total idiot. Instead, Kishan proposes and Kelsey says yes.<br><br>She. Says. Yes.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380353443ra/706790.gif" width="500" height="211" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I don’t think that Kelsey understands what being engaged means. Let me clarify: <br><blockquote>
  <i>2 having formally agreed to marry.</i>
</blockquote><br>Being a fiancée means you should love them unconditionally, and only them - because how are you supposed to live with someone, probably for the rest of your life, and have children and grow old with him, when you’ve been in love with another since you accepted? Being a fiancée is not as simple as being a girlfriend - YOU ARE GETTING MARRIED. I’ll repeat it for you: KELSEY, YOU ARE GOING TO BE HUSBAND AND WIFE, SO WHY THE HELL ARE YOU MARRYING SOMEONE YOU’RE NOT IN LOVE WITH. You should love them! YOU SHOULD LOVE THE PERSON YOU ARE MARRYING IN A ROMANTIC WAY.<br><br>Kelsey is too fucking immature to realize what this means.<br><br><a href="http://photobucket.com/images/i%20hate%20you%20gifs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380353443ra/706791.gif" alt="no words. i hate you Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Of course, Kelsey is actually in love with Ren, but she constantly says she can’t be with him because he’d sacrifice himself for her. She continuously denies her love for Ren, because she's trying 'save him'. She <i>uses Kishan</i> so Ren won't kill himself saving her. He's her rebound, her replacement for not being able to have Ren.<br><br>USER.<br><br>Oh, the tears of irony are leaking from my face. Kishan has sacrificed himself for Kelsey in more important ways, you stupid, stupid girl. <br><br>She spends most of the book shooting Ren longing looks and having steamy conversations with Ren that I swear were written to sound dirty on purpose - here's two:<br><blockquote>
  <i>"To properly ride a horse, you have to form a bond, feel his strength, the power in his muscles. Pay attention to his gait, his stride. Close your eyes. Can you feel how his body rises and falls? He'll take you wherever you want to go. All you need to do is learn to work with him and not against him."</i>
</blockquote><br>and my personal favorite,<br><blockquote>
  <i>"I used the Rope to whip her [the cat]," Ren said.</i>
</blockquote><br>Kelsey also throws various tantrums, spewing with venom, all centered around Ren and his possible relationship with Anamika (the Clan leader destined to stop Lokesh in the past), when she has absolutely no fucking right.<br><br>If someone was in love with you, and you decided to marry someone else, would it make any sense for you to be furious with the person you left after you see them with someone else? NO IT DOES NOT.<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/no%20gifs/SuperJazz24/Gifs/RetardAlert.gif?o=3" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380353443ra/706792.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I really should have bet money on who’d get Kelsey, though, because, damn. I would’ve made a lot. It couldn’t have been more obvious, but it still stung like a bitch.<br><br>The love triangle was no doubt the worst part of the book. Kelsey has an easy life if the biggest problem she faces is having two yummy guys in love with her - because let's face it. If Kishan only thought of her as a friend, she wouldn't look twice at him.<br><br><b>Characters</b><br><br>I think we've already established Kelsey is one of the worst protagonists ever, no? And that Ren and Kishan are unrecognizable, as they've changed themselves for Kelsey?<br><br>Here, I mainly want to clap and thank <s>Durga</s>Anamika. Anamika, who reminds me so much of my dearest Asami, in personality and looks. Anamika, who is actually Durga but doesn't really act like it. Anamika, who constantly tortured Kelsey until she finally decided to like her. -.- Dammit.<br><br><b>Ending</b><br>For the very last part of releasing the curse, a tiger must be given to Durga to become Damon, her lover and her co-tiger-person. Guess who’s noble enough to do it? <br><br>Kishan. Kishan, because over and over he’s proved himself to Kelsey, but she continues to run back to Ren when she has more than she needs. <br><br>It was a rushed and horrible ending to a love triangle for an unlikable girl. It felt like Colleen was out of ideas, so she just decided to grab a doll of Kishan and Anamika and do this:<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/now%20kiss/MunchflowerZaius/now-kiss.jpg?o=4" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380353443i/706793.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>It was much too forced. Kishan even writes a letter saying how it took a lot of time for him to get over Kelsey... I just hope he really loves Anamika. <br><br>But I still can't get over how fast Kelsey got over Kishan. In a snap of my fingers (one week, to be exact) Kelsey was getting married to Ren with no regrets. I literally felt nauseous. In seven days I can't get over finishing <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/7977037.Darkness_Falls__Immortal_Beloved___2_" title="Darkness Falls (Immortal Beloved, #2) by Cate Tiernan" rel="nofollow noopener">Darkness Falls</a> and this little harpy is getting married after her fiancée GAVE HIMSELF UP FOR HER.<br><br>Just because your fiancée tells your lover to make sure you're happy doesn't mean you go marry him IN A WEEK.<br><br>THERE IS MORE TO YOUR LIFE THAN GETTING MARRIED, KELSEY. GET YOUR ACT TOGETHER AND THEN THINK OF BECOMING A WIFE, YOU MORON.<br><br><b>Writing</b><br>I suffer from second-hand embarrassment when I read Houck's books. The series uses so many similes and metaphors (mostly during kissing scenes), it makes Cassandra Clare's writing look non-descriptive. In TIGER'S DESTINY, the writing has calmed down, but I still headdesk whenever it gets out of control. <br><br>It's like the steamier the scene (and trust me, it's no steam. It's just way too much flowery writing), the more descriptive the writing gets. I doubt any girl would think the way Kelsey does.<br><br><b>Wrap-up</b><br><br>It was such a disappointing ending (is it an end? Because there's still TIGER'S DREAM, but this sounds like the final book. I think Kelsey's going to be pregnant in the last book, FML, just watch) to the series, and just a plainly disappointing book in all. The series started out amazing and shit hit the fan after Voyage. I was so sad when I finished, because I expected the series to be so much better.<br><br>It left me feeling like this, the most over-used gif ever:<br><br><a href="http://media.photobucket.com/image/sobbing%20gifs/moirafae/macro/gifs/tumblr_lixeousomf1qbg12q.gif?o=26" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380353443ra/706794.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I leave with you with this brilliant quote from the Phoenix directed at Kelsey:<br><blockquote>
  <i>"As it is, you life is rather pathetic. What a waste."</i>
</blockquote></span>
  <a data-text-id="61537549631801160" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

THIS BOOK HAD A GREAT ENDING!!!<br/><br/><br/><br/><b>UPDATE Nov. 22, 2012 </b><br/><br/><b>YOU DON'T KNOW HOW LONG I'VE BEEN WAITING TO READ THIS BOOK. MY COPY FINALLY ARRIVED FROM THE LIBRARY AND I MUST S</b></span>
  <span id="freeText6869226974331796406" style="display:none"><b>UPDATE Nov. 23, 2012 </b><br><br><p>
  <a href="http://photobucket.com/images/sheldon%20gifs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380340288ra/696733.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

  <a href="http://photobucket.com/images/sheldon%20gifs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/352620.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</p><br><br><b>ALKDGJILDSKAJLAKDIS I DON'T KNOW HOW I CAN LIVE ANYMORE!!!! MY EMOTIONS, THE FEELINGS, THE OMG WHAT DID I JUST READ???? COLLEEN HOUCK YOU HAVE UTTERLY RUINED MY LIFE WITH THE MOST AMAZING, HEART-ACHING, EMOTIONAL ROLLER COASTER, AND BEAUTIFUL BOOK EVER.</b><br><br>BUT WHY IS THERE A FIFTH BOOK?!?!?! THIS BOOK HAD A GREAT ENDING!!!<br><br><br><br><b>UPDATE Nov. 22, 2012 </b><br><br><b>YOU DON'T KNOW HOW LONG I'VE BEEN WAITING TO READ THIS BOOK. MY COPY FINALLY ARRIVED FROM THE LIBRARY AND I MUST SAY, ALOT CAN HAPPEN IN THE FIRST 50 PAGES OF A BOOK (this book particularly) </b><br><br><br><br>THE COVER LOOKS AMAZING! NOW I REALLY CAN'T WAIT UNTIL TO READ IT!<br><br>After reading Tiger's Voyage I was like:<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380372195ra/725430.gif" width="300" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>And after finally getting over the trauma I've experienced from the ending of Tiger's Voyage, I waited for the cover for Tiger's Destiny. And after seeing the cover, I am now like this:<br><br><p>
  <a href="http://photobucket.com/images/sheldon%20gifs" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380298378ra/683019.gif" alt="Hyperventilating Sheldon Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</p><br><br><br>To be honest, I can't wait, I NEED THIS BOOK NOW!!!! I NEED TO KNOW WHAT HAPPENS!!!! <br><br>Please be released faster, please :'(</span>
  <a data-text-id="6869226974331796406" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_200017877" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/200017877" />
    <a title="Katie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3736122-katie"><img alt="Katie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1524600311p2/3736122.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/200017877?book_show_action=true">Aug 18, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katie" href="/user/show/3736122-katie">Katie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3736122-katie?shelf=i-ship-it">i-ship-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3736122-katie?shelf=mythology">mythology</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3736122-katie?shelf=time-travel">time-travel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3736122-katie?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer200017877" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9861226956670604061">Similar Books: None that I can think of - this series is something very different than what else is out there in the market.<br/><br/><b>Real Rating:</b> 3 1/2 stars<br/><br/>This is a hard review for me to write, y'all. I LOVED the first two books in this series. They were like nothing else I'd read, and I couldn't get enough. I loved that Colleen Houck was writing about something you don't see much in YA - Eastern mythology - but even the wicked mythology couldn't save this one for me, unfortunately.<br/><br/>First, let's talk ab</span>
  <span id="freeText9861226956670604061" style="display:none">Similar Books: None that I can think of - this series is something very different than what else is out there in the market.<br><br><b>Real Rating:</b> 3 1/2 stars<br><br>This is a hard review for me to write, y'all. I LOVED the first two books in this series. They were like nothing else I'd read, and I couldn't get enough. I loved that Colleen Houck was writing about something you don't see much in YA - Eastern mythology - but even the wicked mythology couldn't save this one for me, unfortunately.<br><br>First, let's talk about the awesome things in this book:<br><br><b>1.</b> The pacing of this novel was so much better than the other 3. I remember buying <i>Tiger's Voyage</i> and gaping at the size of it. I mean, it could kill someone if you threw it at them. And the pacing of the first 3 books was laborious at times (although I'll be honest and say that it didn't bug me to read about all their meals and Kelsey's clothes - wasn't so good for my diet, though), but this one starts with a bang, keeps up the intensity, and ends with one too. I think people who found the first 3 slow will prefer this book's pacing.<br><br><b>2.</b> THE COVER!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380357217ra/708554.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's so pretty that it almost hurts my eyes. Splinter design team, I am very impressed.<br><br><b>3.</b> I thought Houck handled the "chosen one" plot very well. Usually, I'm not into that kinda thing. (It's actually what kept me from loving <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/172032573" rel="nofollow noopener">Shadow and Bone</a> by Leigh Bardugo.) But I think the fact that Ren, Kishan, and Kelsey all have a specific destiny was what made me prefer that plot device - the destiny, chosen one-ness was sort of shared all around, and that felt more natural.<br><br><b>4.</b> To everyone that thought Kelsey was TSTL in book(s) 1 (and maybe 2), I give you kickbutt Kelsey who most certainly can take care of herself. I mean...wow. She turned into Zena, Warrior Princess in this book. This is another thing that sorta irks me - average girls turning into these Amazon warriors, but I actually totally bought it in this book...probably because of the supernatural assistance she got.<br><br><b>5.</b> A lot of times in paranormal books, we get frustrated with characters who are in mortal danger but they talk about their feelings and get all romantic instead of worrying about how they're going to defend themselves. But this book wasn't like that AT ALL! There's not talking about feelings or any smooshiness when battle approaches. I liked that a lot!<br><br>Okay...nos for what I didn't care for as much.<br><br>OMG THE ROMANCE!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380357217ra/708555.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I like love triangles. I do. No, really. Edward/Jacob? Loved it. Peeta/Gale? Loved it. But Ren/Kishan? At first, I was really into it. But at this point, I'm over it.<br><br>Because there was so much quick pacing in this book, I felt like the character development really suffered. Kelsey, Ren, and Kishan really stay the same throughout this book - nothing changes in any of their relationships, no growth, no nothing. I wanted Ren and Kishan to FINALLY just come to the point where they can't stand each other anymore or they realize that Kelsey isn't worth fighting over. I wanted Kelsey to MAKE UP HER MIND. I wanted Kishan to see Kelsey mooning over Ren and be like, "Eff this. I'm done with you."<br><br>Unfortunately, none of this happened. It was just lots of angst and stolen glances between Kelsey and Ren...even after <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Kishan PROPOSES and Kelsey SAYS YES!!!!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380357217ra/708556.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>I get it now - the Kelsey/Ren thing. In <i>Voyage</i> I fought it because I just didn't understand why she would ever want to be with Ren while Kishan was around. But after reading <i>Destiny</i>, I can see that for whatever reason, she's into him and it's better for her to be with him instead of Kishan. I still don't get why any sane person would want to be with a guy that's so dramatic and angsty that he literally throws himself at your feet and begs you not to do something dangerous when THAT'S THE WHOLE POINT OF YOUR JOURNEY...but I digress.<br><br>The end. OMG the end.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/306174.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We all know what's going to happen. <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Durga needs a tiger, and Kishan will volunteer to be said tiger. Because Houck has been hinting at it from the beginning, with the way Durga shamelessly flirts with him. Because Kishan has proved himself throughout the entire series to be the most noble out of the three main characters. Because Kelsey is an idiot who doesn't realize a good thing when she has it. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>But all I have to say is...<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380357217ra/708557.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So many FEELS, guys. So many.<br><br><br>But at the end of the day, I'm just impressed with an author who can make me have that many feels. Colleen Houck has really done an incredible job of creating these characters that are really well-rounded and actualized, that readers fall in love with.<br><br>I love this story that she's crafted. It's pretty epic. Like in the literal sense. I applaud her for the amount of research that she's done, for writing something that nobody else is really doing, and for being basically awesome incarnate.<br><br>...but I just can't give your book 5 stars when you screw over my favorite character.<br><br>In defense of Kishan, I knock off 1 1/2 stars.</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="9861226956670604061" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_611876264" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/611876264" />
    <a title="Mizuki" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16842102-mizuki"><img alt="Mizuki" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368277474p2/16842102.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/611876264?book_show_action=true">May 10, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mizuki" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mizuki" href="/user/show/16842102-mizuki">Mizuki</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=would-not-read-it-anytime-soon">would-not-read-it-anytime-soon</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=are-you-kidding-me">are-you-kidding-me</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=bad-bad-bad-romance">bad-bad-bad-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=over-my-dead-body">over-my-dead-body</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=no-hell-no">no-hell-no</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=chinese-translation">chinese-translation</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=young-adult-books">young-adult-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=i-hate-love-triangle">i-hate-love-triangle</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=supernatural-stuff">supernatural-stuff</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16842102-mizuki?shelf=unrealistic-main-characters">unrealistic-main-characters</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer611876264" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11544178407031942076"><b>Rating: Actually it should be a negative-20 stars, but Goodread wouldn't allow this rating so I made do with one star. It's easily one of the worst books I've ever read in my life.</b><br/><br/><b>Warning: F-words flying from all directions, don't like don't read.</b><br/><br/>To: <s>Dear</s> Colleen Houck<br/>From: Mizuki<br/><br/>Hello, Colleen Houck.<br/><br/>I'd decided to skip those 'dear this' and 'dear that' because to be frank, <i>I have no respect toward you as an 'author' and I don't really think you deserve to be called one.</i> Still for the sake of bo</span>
  <span id="freeText11544178407031942076" style="display:none"><b>Rating: Actually it should be a negative-20 stars, but Goodread wouldn't allow this rating so I made do with one star. It's easily one of the worst books I've ever read in my life.</b><br><br><b>Warning: F-words flying from all directions, don't like don't read.</b><br><br>To: <s>Dear</s> Colleen Houck<br>From: Mizuki<br><br>Hello, Colleen Houck.<br><br>I'd decided to skip those 'dear this' and 'dear that' because to be frank, <i>I have no respect toward you as an 'author' and I don't really think you deserve to be called one.</i> Still for the sake of both literature and humanity, I would like to suggest you to do a couple of things:<br><b><br>(1) Next time, when you write books about foreign cultures and societies, DO YOUR FXXKING RESEARCH. DO YOUR HOMEWORK.<br><br>(2) Next time, when you include Eastern mythologies in your books, DO NOT insert an ignorant White Girl who knows nothing about said mythologies and let said White Girl become the savior of all creatures. It's goddamn offensive.<br><br>(3) Take a goddamn writing lesson before you start writing anything else again. Pretty, please.<br><br>(4) DO NOT mix different cultures and mythical creatures from different mythologies together like they're one great big fucking happy family, for no explanation and no good reason.<br><br>(5) DO NOT insert a White Skinned Mary Sue, who is even bigger a Mary Sue than Bella freaking Swan from Twilight, into your story.<br><br>(6) Myths and history ARE NOT THE SAME THING. Get it!?<br><br>(7) For God's sake, BE RESPECTFUL to other people's cultures and traditions. DON'T MAKE THINGS UP, JUST DON'T. Okay?<br><br>(8) If you really, really need to make things up, CREATE YOUR OWN MYTH, BUILD YOUR OWN FANTASY WORLD instead of inserting your make-believe bullshit into someone else's myths and cultures. No one needs to have their cultures shitted all over like what you had done with Hindus/Chinese myths and history.<br></b><br><br>None of the above is so very difficult to do, right?<br><br>Right now, all I can say about Tiger's Destiny is: <b>The only thing which is worse than the first 300 pages of this book, is the last 100 pages of this book.</b><br><br>When I was in the middle of the book, I kept telling myself <i>"Colleen Houck had already done her worst in the previous books, I'm NOT going to get angry because of this last book and its stupidity. I'm not going to throw a bitch fit over the stupidity, I'm not going to throw a bitch fit over the <b>FUCKING STUPIDITY!!!</b>"</i><br><br>But in the ending, I was very, very angry and I did throw my bitch fit, because the ending part of Tight's Destiny is just ridiculously, eye-poppingly, outrageously BAD. <br><br>And here's my feeling to this so-called Tiger Saga as a whole...<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388139726i/7747248._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(LINK: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jpopasia.com/forums/posts-in/artist-angelo::20::11494::1?p=2">http://www.jpopasia.com/forums/posts-...</a>)<br><br><i> Pre-Review: </i><br><br>In my Tiger's Voyage review (<a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://vampirekiki.deviantart.com/art/Book-Review-Tiger-s-Voyage-by-Colleen-Houck-369615279?q=gallery%3Avampirekiki&amp;qo=3">http://vampirekiki.deviantart.com/art...</a>), I made comments how Colleen Houck failed to mention realistic details about Indian's society, such as:<br><br>(1) Houck did not mention seeing any poor people, or one single beggar on the street. Instead she made it sound like every single person who lived in India was rich or at the very least, middle class.<br><br>(2) It's barely noted that how hot the weather can be, with all the rain and stuff...<br><br>(3) Not once did she mention anything about the social/cultural barriers between Indian men and women, nor did any of her characters seem to notice romantic relationship and marriage are being viewed in ways which are quite different from American/Western societies. <br><br>Now I have something to add:<br><br>(4) Houck did not mention anything about cows, monkeys or other animals wandering on the streets. Yes, since India is still partly an rural society, plus cows and a handful of other animals are being viewed as holy, so animals DO wandering on the streets, even in the largest cities. <br><br>Well, I think these are things that you would have paid your attention to.<br><br>(5) Not once did she mention the untidiness in some parts of the cities/towns/villages/places her characters had visited. Instead Houck made it sound like the environment in India doesn't have much difference with America. <br><br>Oh well, those Bollywood movies always want to have you believed that India is ALL MIDDLE CLASS, ALL WESTERNIZED, ALL CLEAN AND MODERN. But, it really isn't the whole picture.<br><br>Houck, I have to wonder how can you fail in so many ways.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421066i/836061._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I won't keep my hope up.<br><br><br><b>Update of reading progress:</b><br><br>First I want to talk about Houck's 'poems'. Yes, she added at least two poems of hers into the book.<br><br>And here's my suggestion for all authors and wannabe-authors out there: <b>If you were going to quote Lord Tennyson's and Edgar Allan Poe's poems in your book, then DO NOT add your own crappy poems in the same book!</b> It only makes your bad poems look even worse when we compare your crappy poems with Lord Tennyson's and Poe's!<br><br>Secondly, about 50 pages into the book, I am faced with Colleen Houck screwing up Chinese history *again*.<br><br>We're told that supposedly, the villain was the bastard son of an emperor of the ancient Chinese Shu kingdom (also known as Shu Han <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shu_Han">http://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Shu_Han</a> ), and his mother was supposed to be an Indian slave girl. The time of the villain's birth was probably somewhere between 221 AD to 263 AD.<br><br>I will not even bother to tell you there's no historical record for that supposed bastard son between the Shu Emperor and an Indian slave (a royal bastard went unnoticed? how likely can it be?). I wouldn't even bother. Still, ladies and gentlemen, I would like to inform you that at the time of the Three Kingdoms era, China was a much smaller country than its current self, and I would also like to show you a map of China from the Three Kingdoms era.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421066i/836062.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(Note: the map is taken from Wiki)<br><br>So you can see the Kingdom of Shu on the map, you can also see its two warring neighbors: Kingdom of Wei and Kingdom of Wu, you can also see Korea and Taiwan on the map, but can you see India?<br><br>Well, of course you can't see India anywhere near Kingdom of Shu, because geographically these two kingdoms were so far, far apart! You can imagine how difficult it would be to transport Indian slaves all the way to the Shu realm.<br><br>Then, would somebody tells me how did Shu Emperor import Indian slaves?<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380421066i/836063.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>At around page. 60, Kelsey needed to learn more things about the birth of Goddess Durga, so she went to read some books---not that I have any objection on her doing some research; but then the next thing we know, Kelsey was lecturing the Durga myth to both Ren and Kishan. I AM SORRY? Shouldn't these two Indian princes know the Durga myth by heart!? For crying out loud, Durga is one of the most popular goddesses in India and her many myths are well known. So why must two Indians learn about their own mythology from the White Girl? Colleen Houck, you must be kidding.<br><br>I need to tell you I have serious issues with the ending of Tiger's Destiny. I was enraged when Houck basically tells us through out the centuries, all Indians have gotten the Durga Myths all wrong, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Goddess Durga actually didn't defeat the great bull demon by herself, instead the bull demon was taken down by a White Girl Who Has The Power Of A Goddess!? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Words can't describe how angry I felt when I read this bullshit.<br><br><i>Updated@22/07/2014:</i><br><br>*facepalms* and now it's confirmed that Houck has never visited India *at all*.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1405999198i/10484318.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>(LINK: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://s64.photobucket.com/user/Teklafall/media/tiger-related%20quotes/googlemaps_zpsce76b47c.png.html">http://s64.photobucket.com/user/Tekla...</a>)<br><br><b> detailed rant to come...I guess.</b></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_245862606" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/245862606" />
    <a title="Lucy Qhuay" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7115693-lucy-qhuay"><img alt="Lucy Qhuay" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1564407818p2/7115693.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/245862606?book_show_action=true">Dec 11, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lucy Qhuay" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lucy Qhuay" href="/user/show/7115693-lucy-qhuay">Lucy Qhuay</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">people who love to suffer</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7115693-lucy-qhuay?shelf=young-adult-series">young-adult-series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7115693-lucy-qhuay?shelf=covergasm">covergasm</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7115693-lucy-qhuay?shelf=best-villains-ever">best-villains-ever</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7115693-lucy-qhuay?shelf=heroes-to-die-for">heroes-to-die-for</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7115693-lucy-qhuay?shelf=characters-i-wanna-bitch-slap">characters-i-wanna-bitch-slap</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7115693-lucy-qhuay?shelf=sexy-bad-boys">sexy-bad-boys</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7115693-lucy-qhuay?shelf=too-much-fucking-drama">too-much-fucking-drama</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7115693-lucy-qhuay?shelf=emotional-roller-coaster">emotional-roller-coaster</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7115693-lucy-qhuay?shelf=everyone-loves-a-tortured-hero">everyone-loves-a-tortured-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7115693-lucy-qhuay?shelf=i-died">i-died</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer245862606" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11007213721000788631"><b> Sorry for all the profanity and spoilers you will read from now on! </b><br/><br/>That being said...<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380364756ra/716544.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I am sitting here wondering why the fuck did Colleen Houck do something like this to me and to all the fans of this series.<br/>Tiger Saga was one of my favourite series. Ever. And now the calamity that is this book happened and I know things will never be the same.<br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380364756ra/716545.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I tell you, never in my life have I cursed so much as while I was reading Tiger's Destiny!--'<br/>And why did I curse so much? Because of several things, my </span>
  <span id="freeText11007213721000788631" style="display:none"><b> Sorry for all the profanity and spoilers you will read from now on! </b><br><br>That being said...<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380364756ra/716544.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I am sitting here wondering why the fuck did Colleen Houck do something like this to me and to all the fans of this series.<br>Tiger Saga was one of my favourite series. Ever. And now the calamity that is this book happened and I know things will never be the same.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380364756ra/716545.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I tell you, never in my life have I cursed so much as while I was reading Tiger's Destiny!--'<br>And why did I curse so much? Because of several things, my dear friends, but especially because of the so called heroine, Kelsey fucking Hayes!<br>She really pissed me the fuck off! -.-'<br>I swear I tried to understand what the fuck was going on in that little head of hers but I couldn't.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380364756ra/716546.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I couldn't understand why, if you love someone, would you be with someone else. I couldn't understand why, if your love is so strong, wouldn't you be able to choose between the person you love and the other one. I couldn't understand why would you subject your beloved to so much misery.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380364756ra/716547.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Kelsey's behavior was despicable! Outrageous!<br>She kept denying Ren and his feelings, railed his love and said that she didn't want to be with him and that she loved Kishan. <br>So, why the fuck didn't she gave him a little rest? Why the fuck did she seek him when he wanted to be alone?<br>Did she want him to sit there and watch all day the sad circus that was Kishan and her cuddling and all lovey lovey and shit? o.O<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380364756ra/716548.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Ren suffered terribly! He came to the point of saying that he almost preferred to be tortured again by Lokesh, rather than continue like that!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/361727.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>So, if she was so set on being with Kishan, the least she could do was leave Ren alone.<br>But no! The bitch had to be all over Kishan and then when everybody bailed on her and she didn't want to be alone, she would go see where Ren was.<br>The fucking bitch was torturing the one and only person that loves her the most in the fucking planet. She was hurting him, in every way possible, even physically, but she didn't care. <br>She just left him there, hurting, begging! :@<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/365722.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Furthermore, who the fuck did she think she was to have some right to feel angry, annoyed, betrayed, whatever, when Ren just wanted to be alone and, eventually, go on with his life?<br>When she caught him with Anamika she was pissed off and thought that she wanted to plunge a knife into his "unfaithful heart". What the fucking fuck? o.O<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380364756ra/716549.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Excuse the hell out of me, so it is right for you to want both brothers, be with one and terribly hurt the other, but he can't try to keep living without you? o.O<br>Even when he had already said that he couldn't do it?<br>Who has the "unfaithful heart"? Who is the selfish, narcisist slut?<br>But it wasn't just Kelsey that pissed me the fuck off in this book!<br>Let's see:<br>- the entire Saachi situation - I thought that Ren was Saachi but it was Kishan after all. What the fuck? Unless Kishan used the scarf to impersonate Saachi and then Ren.<br>But Colleen tells us that when Kelsey finally admited to Saachi that Ren was the one she really loved, Saachi smiled or whatever in a way that said "I knew it!" or "I told you so!".<br>So, it would be a little weird if it was Kishan acting like that.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380364756ra/716550.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>- Ren's death - Damnit! Ren didn't have to die! I was truly devastated! :'(<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380364756ra/716551.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Also, I was too fucking enraged when Kishan brought him back, not because he was his brother but because he wanted to please his <s> bitch </s> fiancée.<br>- Anamika's/Durga's demeanor - I must say that Durga as a mortal was a little too bitchy and sarcastic to my liking and as a goddess was worthless because she didn't do shit!<br>She was not the one defeating Lokesh. Fucking Kelsey defeated the sucker with Ren's help, of course!<br>- Kishan's end - Why the hell did he have to make a second sacrifice when everybody else just made one? Fuck this!<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/338982.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>It should be Durga making this sacrifice, <s> since she didn't do shit </s> out of the goodness of her goddess heart *cough*!<br>Now, Kishan had to stay in the fucking past to be her <s> sex slave </s> tiger pet.<br>This was so fucked up that I actually cried for him!<br>- the actual end of the book - Things happened too fucking quickly!<br>One moment Kelsey was Kishan's bitch and saying that a part of her would always be Ren's and the other she was with Ren saying that a part of her would always be Kishan's.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380364756ra/716552.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Bipolar bitch! :S<br>And then they were happy and all lovey lovey and married and shit.<br>I was left wondering why the fuck do we need a fifth book if there is not much to say.<br>I guess Tiger's Dream will be about Anik but we'll see.<br>However, I had to give 3 stars to this book for my Ren's sake or otherwise I would feel bad. But I didn't really want to...<br>Anyway, Ren, I love you so much! You're perfetc!<br>Leave Kelsey and we can be happy together! +.+<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/458631.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="11007213721000788631" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_202869510" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/202869510" />
    <a title="Katherine" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4356179-katherine"><img alt="Katherine" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1379922903p2/4356179.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/202869510?book_show_action=true">Aug 27, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katherine" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katherine" href="/user/show/4356179-katherine">Katherine</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4356179-katherine?shelf=dissapointed">dissapointed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4356179-katherine?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4356179-katherine?shelf=magic-powers">magic-powers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4356179-katherine?shelf=mythology-gods">mythology-gods</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer202869510" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1767840585091581163"><u>RATING: 2.5 Out Of 5</u><br/><br/><a href='http://s164.photobucket.com/albums/u13/librachick26/?action=view&current=95c7a296c0f5170b9804224d59c0fc0e-d4p7zan.gif' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380357789ra/709026.gif' alt='Photobucket' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Tiger's Destiny has the same flaws that Tiger's Voyage did. Reading Destiny just made me feel like I was reading Voyage all over again and that really does suck. When this series started with Curse, I was in love, the first novel was AMAZING!! I loved loved loved it and the second novel Quest was just as good, but from there everything went downhill.<br/><br/>There is only so long that readers can read the same thing continuously, there is only so long before the same love triangle</span>
  <span id="freeText1767840585091581163" style="display:none"><u>RATING: 2.5 Out Of 5</u><br><br><a href="http://s164.photobucket.com/albums/u13/librachick26/?action=view&amp;current=95c7a296c0f5170b9804224d59c0fc0e-d4p7zan.gif" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380357789ra/709026.gif" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Tiger's Destiny has the same flaws that Tiger's Voyage did. Reading Destiny just made me feel like I was reading Voyage all over again and that really does suck. When this series started with Curse, I was in love, the first novel was AMAZING!! I loved loved loved it and the second novel Quest was just as good, but from there everything went downhill.<br><br>There is only so long that readers can read the same thing continuously, there is only so long before the same love triangle gets so repetitive and boring. What’s worse with every continuing book in this series I hate and despise Kelsey more and more? She is not a very likeable character, especially after everyone knows she loves Ren but she’s okay with stringing Kishan along continuously. You’re a bitch Kelsey; it’s all I can say. The scene that secured that defection to her is one where she and Kishan are lying on the beach and while he is proposing to her, she’s too busy perving at Rens half naked body! And even know she never sleeps with any of the brother I can’t help think of how much of a whore she is, she jumps back and forth between the two brothers, it’s just..... Cruel.<br><br>But aside from this, what really was the major disappointment with this novel was the plot. It sucked, it was just (again like Voyage) over the top, silly and ridiculous. Too much happened, 50 million things happen in the book that it just felt over packed with stuff and not even good stuff. It just appears that Houck didn’t know what to put into the story and just put a whole bunch of crap in there just to lengthen out then novel.<br><br>What’s even stranger about this novel in particular is that the series is properly ended in this novel, they finish the quests and she ends up with a brother, so why is there another novel???? What could is possibly be about. <br><br>On my Voyage review I stated that Voyage was the weakest book of the three, I can now correct this and say that Destiny is definitely the weakest of the four. Not only this but I stated that hopefully the series will return to its former glory with Destiny - I was wrong. It all went severely down from Voyage and it deeply saddens me to think about where this series first started off being one of the best series I had read and it being amazing (book 1 and 2) to having such crappy books to follow it and end with, it’s just not right. You see this quite alot with authors who have such great ideas and concepts with novels and their novels start off fantastically, but as the series progresses it appears obvious to readers that the author doesn’t know where to take their story and struggles to come up with books to top its first novels in the series; Hunger Games, Strange Angels.. Are just to name a few. <br><br>Sooo disappointed....<br><br>But here is an awesome picture I found by ~Juhani of Ren &amp; Kelsey<br><a href="http://s164.photobucket.com/albums/u13/librachick26/?action=view&amp;current=untitled.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380357789i/709027._SY540_.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://juhani.deviantart.com/art/Kelsey-and-Ren-294683233">http://juhani.deviantart.com/art/Kels...</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="1767840585091581163" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_308594376" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/308594376" />
    <a title="Itzel " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7789356-itzel"><img alt="Itzel " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1484554003p2/7789356.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/308594376?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Itzel " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Itzel " href="/user/show/7789356-itzel">Itzel </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer308594376" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17113955817882797364"><b>
  <i>Warning:</i>
</b> There will be <u>spoilers, angry ranting, and profanity in this review. If you are not comfortable with any of these, and loved the book down to every single word, I highly suggest you don't read my review.</u><br/><br/>I can't even begin to describe how much I <b>hated</b> this book. It hurts me to say this because I <i>loved</i> the first two book, but this book was just a complete disaster from start to finish. I actually threw the book <b>several</b> times, and screamed at Kelsey- who was the problem ninety-nine per</span>
  <span id="freeText17113955817882797364" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>Warning:</i>
</b> There will be <u>spoilers, angry ranting, and profanity in this review. If you are not comfortable with any of these, and loved the book down to every single word, I highly suggest you don't read my review.</u><br><br>I can't even begin to describe how much I <b>hated</b> this book. It hurts me to say this because I <i>loved</i> the first two book, but this book was just a complete disaster from start to finish. I actually threw the book <b>several</b> times, and screamed at Kelsey- who was the problem ninety-nine percent of the time. <br><br>I <b>made</b> a list of the things I hated in this book, and had to <u>condense</u> the list into nine things. There was a lot I wanted to add on the list, but I stopped myself from writing an entire book. <br><br><b>The List</b><br><br>1.<b>KELSEY</b><br><br>2. Ren<br><br>3. Lokesh<br><br>4. The Writing<br><br>5. The LOTR/Narnia battle scenes<br><br>6. The Love Triangle<br><br>7. Mr. Kadam's death<br><br>8. Kishan and his decision in the end<br><br>9. The ending<br><br><br><br><br><br><br><br>1. Kelsey<br><br>The first on the list <b>had</b> to be Kelsey. It just had to be her. She was manipulative, jealous, and constantly needed to saved because she was too precious. There was also the fact that every male in the whole fucking universe wanted her. I can count all the men who wanted to be her if you don't believe me. <br><br>Here we go. <br><br>Artie <br><br>Wes <br><br>Li<br><br>Kishan <br><br>Ren <br><br>Lokesh <br><br>Lighting<br><br>Wyeas<br><br>Shala<br><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/view/2237145/really-bitch.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a> <br><br>You've got to be fucking me, that is way too many suitors lusting after Kelsey. The author is basically writing on Kelsey's forehead Mary-sue. And the interesting thing is that Kelsey is boring, stupid and selfish. <br><br>How can men find her at least a bit attractive is beyond me. I wanted to dive inside this book and grab Kelsey by the shoulders, and shake her hard. Most of the time, she's overly dependent on Ren and Kishan that she can't do anything by herself. In the beginning, she's trapped by Lokesh. Kelsey <i>tries</i> to manipulate Lokesh but ends up looking stupid. <br><br>Lokesh, on the other hand, was the stereotypical villain who has to have the girl, and blah blah blah. I'll get more into that later. Anyway, Kelsey agrees to marry Lokesh. In the meantime, the audience is told how its <b>IMPOSSIBLE</b> to infiltrate the place where Kelsey been kidnapped to and how its impossible to escape.<br><br>But somehow during their wedding, Ren and Kishan appear out of nowhere and stop the wedding. Wait hold the fuck up! <br><br>You just said that its IMPOSSIBLE to get inside this place, but somehow the two brothers disguised themselves and successfully got inside. How does this make any sense whatsoever. I just couldn't understand this. You just contradicted yourself. <br><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/view/2502107/what-the-fuck-xd.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <span>[image error]</span>
</a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a><br><br>After this stupidity, Kelsey gets rescued and their off to their next quest. The transition between these two points was horribly written and rushed. <br><br>During their next quest, Kelsey is still in a relationship with Kishan, but her heart yearns for Ren. This also bothered me A LOT. How can Kelsey be so selfish and stupid. Early in the book she realizes that she's still in love with Ren, and Ren finds out about it. Then she does the following.<br><br>Ren:<i>I wanted to know. I needed to know. You've kept all your true feelings from the both of us. Kelsey, why didn't you share these worries? These fears?"</i> <br><br>Kelsey:<i>"Would it have changed anything? Does it make a difference?"</i><br><br>Ren:<i>"I don't know. Maybe. Maybe not. But at least all the cards are on the table now." <br><br>Kelsey:<i>I bit my lip. "Are you going to tell him?"</i> <br><br>Ren:<i>"Don't you think he has to know?"</i> <br><br>Me:<i>"YES, HE HAS THE RIGHT TO KNOW!"</i><br><br>Kelsey:<i>"I don't see how it will help."</i><br><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/view/30604/bitch-slap.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span>[image error]</span></a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a><br><br>Fuck you, Kelsey. Fuck you. <br><br>I wanted to slap Kelsey in the face right then and there. How <b>DARE</b> she say she doesn't see how it could help. She's deceiving a poor man and leading on his feelings when she isn't really in love with him. How low of her to even say that, and for Ren to keep quiet about this was cowardly of him. Kelsey deserved a slap. If only I were in that book, I'll do it without thinking twice.<br><br>Then she has the audacity to accept Kishan's proposal, and at the same time he's proposing, she's fucking staring at Ren. She accepts of course, and Ren flees. After accepting Kishan, she feels like her heart is breaking, and how she wants to be really be with Ren not Kishan. <br><br>w/36433/knockout-punch.html" target="_blank"&gt;<span>[image error]</span><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a><br><br><b>THEN WHY THE FUCK DID YOU ACCEPT HIS PROPOSAL, KELSEY! WHY?!</b><br><br>After this, every single time a woman approaches Ren or even looks at him, Kelsey gets mad at Ren. <br><br>Are fucking shitting me, Kelsey. YOU have no right to talk. You're lying to a man, and deceiving him and yet you sit there, and forbid Ren from starting a new relationship.<br><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/view/66250/facepalm.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span>[image error]</span></a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a><br><br>Kelsey, I won't speak your name anymore. From now on, your name is <i>two-face</i>. It fits you perfectly. <br><br>Through all this unnecessary drama, two-face treats her like a fucking queen. Even Mr. Kadam treats her like a daughter, and completely ignores Nilima. It's absolutely ridiculous. I don't the attraction of two-face, I really don't. Is it because she's pretty because it's mentioned A LOT. But <i>of course, like the true Mary-sue that she is</i> she doesn't know. <br><br>This "thing" where the main character doesn't know that she's beautiful is seriously pissing me off. Ever heard of mirrors? I'm pretty sure anyone can see if there pretty or not. They should a brain that works, unfortunately, two-face doesn't. <br><br>And why is so bad to have a normal-looking girl as the main character? Why does every main character have to be gorgeous, and beautiful? <br><br>There's also the fact that two-face feels that both brothers <i>belong</i> to her. She always says, "my tigers". Mine, mine, mine. Two-face is a two-year old who doesn't want to share her toys. It pissed me off.<br><br>Also, two-face was too dependent on Kishan and Ren. They were two moments where she'll get mad for sitting on the sidelines, and say she'll fight with them, and I was slightly happy. But in the end, she still sits on the sidelines waiting for the men to do all the work. <br><br>The last straw I had with two-face was when she met Durga, and called her an Amazon. Seriously, two-face. I've had enough of you. You're unnamed now. Several times does she call her a Amazon, and I found it <b>EXTREMELY</b> rude. I wouldn't like to be called Mexican. I have a name too, thank you very much.<br><br>Then unnamed gets mad because Durga is beautiful.<br><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/view/2160586/rage-meter.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span>[image error]</span></a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a> <br><br>Grow the fuck up, unnamed. <br><br><br><br><br>2. Ren<br><br>Ren, in the third book turned into a asshole, plain and simple. In this book, he was sweet at times, then he would turn into that asshole again. He would say that he accepted two-face decision, then the next second, he would throw a tantrum. This got old fast.<br><br>Ren could gone with Durga, and started a relationship, but no. He waited for two-face, and wrote poetry to her. He was also overprotective to the extreme. He constantly growled at everything. And he treated tow-face like a child. <br><br>"Don't do that! You'll get hurt. I'll do it for you." <br><br>Fuck, Ren just stop it. She's a grown-ass woman, she can do it herself. Still, she accepts this treatment.<br><br>But the thing I hated was when he told her that she was his only one, and that they belonged together, and all the corny shit. Then the next scene, he's kissing Durga. <br><br>Wait, what!<br><br>view/225<a href="http://gifsoup.com/6971/liar.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span>[image error]</span></a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a><br><br>Liar. <br><br><br><br><br>3. Lokesh<br><br>Lokesh was the typically bad guy. He was evil, did evil stuff, and had absolutely no depth. He was just evil. It's not explained why he's evil, he just is evil. <br><br>And when he died, I was like, "That's it." <br><br>Towards the end, he turned into a half-demon. He even had horns. I was utterly bored with him.<br><br><br><br>4. The Writing/Plot <br><br>The writing was bad. I mean, really bad. The font distracted me many times, and the writing left much to be desired. Also, there was too much "telling," and not enough, "showing". No name's thoughts often drifted from what was going on. Like I mentioned earlier, the font was huge. I felt like I was reading a picture book. And the pacing was too fast. We barely had time to accept some events before something else happened.<br><br>As for the time traveling device, it completely took me by surprise. <br><br><br><br>5. The Narnia/LOTR battle scenes <br><br>The previous sentence should be self-explanatory. Animals and even the famous elephants fought in the battle. And I swear, I saw these movies playing in head. It is completely unoriginal. I was tempted to skip these pages.<br><br><br><br><br>6. The Love Triangle<br><br>This over-used plot device was forced and cliche to the extreme. I didn't understand why no name couldn't be with Ren. In the end, the author tries to create more drama by putting Durga in the mix. No name being the immature brat that she was, destroyed Durga's belongings, and ran away to cry alone. If I were Durga, I would've slapped her. <br><br>As for Kishan, he got nothing. And we all KNEW, everyone one of us knew that no name would stay with Ren. It was a no brainier. And frankly, I annoyed that the author dragged it out to the end. <br><br>Kishan was only person in the whole love triangle-octagon to lose everything. Seriously, he got the bad end of the deal. No girl, no brother, returned to the past, no longer immoral. Poor guy. <br><br>Either way, the love triangle caused me to scream and throw the book at the wall. <br><br><br><br><br>7. Mr. Kadam's death<br><br>He didn't deserve to die, he didn't. After Kishan, he's my favorite character, and for him to die, I was done with this book. How can you kill off one of the characters who actually use their brain? <br><br>I'm so done with this series. <br><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/view/2818090/shake-head.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span>[image error]</span></a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a> <br><br><br><br><br>8. Kishan and his decision<br><br>As I stated previously, Kishan didn't deserve what he got in the end. I don't believe for one second that he fell in love with Durga. That's such bullshit. I feel the author did the letter to tell us that he's supposedly happy with his life. I'm sorry I don't accept that. If anyone deserved a happy ending, it was Kishan. <br><br>I was really mad he couldn't fall in love on his own, because his falling in love with Durga felt too forced. The last time we saw him, he couldn't stand the sight of her. So, falling in love with her was a huge long shot, and completely unbelievable to me. <br><br><br><br><br>9. The Ending <br><br><br>When I was in elementary school, my mother used to watch Telenovelas, which are Spanish speaking soap operas. Anyway, <b>every SINGLE</b> ending for each telenovela I saw there was a wedding. It didn't matter what the story was, but every single ending, someone was marrying.<br><br>I felt the same with this ending. The wedding was a week after Kishan got left in the past. That was way too fast in my opinion. <br><br>Why does marriage even have to be a option? There both young, they can both travel the world. It seems these days that if you're not married with your partner, that somehow is looked down in this society. <br><br><br><br><br>There is going to be sequel, and I am not going to read it when it first comes out. I'll wait some time before I can forgive no name because right now, I want to strangle her. And without my favorite characters, I don't think I can survive being in no name's head for that long. <br><br>Overall, this book was a cliche mess with a main character I wanted to slap constantly, and a love triangle that was stupid and unnecessary.<br><br>As of right now, I'm done with this series. <br><br>i<a href="http://gifsoup.com/view/2625864/fuck-ths-im-out.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span>[image error]</span></a><br><a href="http://gifsoup.com/" title="GIFSoup" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">GIFSoup</a> <br><br></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="17113955817882797364" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781444757521" href="/book/show/15841110-tiger-s-destiny">review of another edition</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer1769847766461977664"><br/>Summary<br/><br/>With three of the goddess Durga's quests behind them, only one prophecy now stands in the way of Kelsey, Ren, and Kishan breaking the tiger's curse. But the trio's greatest challenge awaits them: A life-endangering pursuit in search of Durga's final gift, the Rope of Fire, on the Andaman Islands in the Bay of Bengal. It's a race against time--and the evil sorcerer Lokesh<br/><br/>Wow!! ...Just wow! This book is amazing, Colleen has done it again, just blown me away with the sheer ...awesome-ness - </span>
  <span id="freeText1769847766461977664" style="display:none"><br />Summary<br /><br />With three of the goddess Durga's quests behind them, only one prophecy now stands in the way of Kelsey, Ren, and Kishan breaking the tiger's curse. But the trio's greatest challenge awaits them: A life-endangering pursuit in search of Durga's final gift, the Rope of Fire, on the Andaman Islands in the Bay of Bengal. It's a race against time--and the evil sorcerer Lokesh<br /><br />Wow!! ...Just wow! This book is amazing, Colleen has done it again, just blown me away with the sheer ...awesome-ness - is that a word? - *shrugs* anyway, TD is such a emotional rollercoster I couldn't stop the tears flowing. I'm not going to give you any spoilers, but there are so many shocks and suprises in store, my advice? prepare yourself! <br /><br />The only negative points are that; The book was too short, there was so much crammed into it, that it felt quite rushed. And after some reflection I'm giving it 4 stars because I felt It just wasn't as good as the 3 previous books. But still a great book! <br /><br />Now for some teasers! <br /><br />"That's what I am, I'm as rotten on the outside as I am on the inside. I'm a power hungry girl from the future who craves the love of two brothers and wants to keep all the magic too."<br /><br />"A devoted heart can overcome any obstacle, rajkumari. Believe that I will keep you safe."<br /><br /><br />I'm now desperate for Tiger's Dream!! I want it so badly! Pwease write fast Colleen, pwetty pwease! :D</span>
